***бревно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бревно.html>бревно</a> (2647)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">бьрьвьно</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bĭrĭvĭno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bьrvьno</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бревно.html>бревно́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">brevnó</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бревно.html>бревна́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бревно.html>брёвна</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бревно.html>брёвен</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>log, beam (trunk of dead tree, cleared of branches)
<ul><li><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white">Александр Солженицын, <i>Матренин <a href = vnd.unilang:двор.html>двор</a></i> 1968:<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посереть.html>посере́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:старость.html>ста́рости</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бревно.html>брёвна</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сруб.html>сру́ба</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ворот.html>во́рота</a>, когда́-то <a href = vnd.unilang:могучий.html>могу́чие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> прореди́лась <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>их</a> обве́ршка</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">poseréli ot stárosti <b>brjóvna</b> srúba i vórota, kogdá-to mogúčije, i proredílasʹ ix obvérška</i></dd><dd>the frame <b>beams</b> as the door, once mighty, had grown with much time grey and its roof had weakened</dd></dl></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lumber</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">gymnastics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> beam, balance beam</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> stupid or heartless man</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dead fish, cold fish <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a very passive sexual partner</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***бред.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бред.html>бред</a> (3323)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бред.html>бред</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bred</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бред.html>бре́да</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>delirium, ravings</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gibberish</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бредень.html>бре́день</a> (20189)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бредень.html>бре́день</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">brédenʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бредень.html>бре́дня</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бредень.html>бре́дни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бредень.html>бре́дней</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">fishing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> small dragnet, seine (for use in shallow water)</li></ol>

***бредить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бредить.html>бре́дить</a> (10983)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бред.html>бред</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bred</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">delirium</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бредить.html>бре́дить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bréditʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to be delirious, to talk deliriously</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to say nonsense</li>
<li>to rave, to be mad about
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бредить.html>бре́дит</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тобо́й</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>brédit</b> tobój.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He is crazy about you.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бредовый.html>бредо́вый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bredóvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">бредя́тина</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bredjátina</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***брезговать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:брезговать.html>бре́зговать</a> (12203)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бре́згать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brézgatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брезговать.html>бре́зговать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">brézgovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побрезговать.html>побре́зговать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be fastidious/squeamish <i>(about)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:брезговать.html>бре́згует</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чужой.html>чужо́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стакан.html>стака́на</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>brézgujet</b> pitʹ iz čužóvo stakána</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is squeamish about drinking out of smb else's glass; it disgusts him to drink out of smb else's glass</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(usually negative)</i> to disdain, to shrink <i>(from)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:брезговать.html>бре́згует</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:никакой.html>никаки́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:средство.html>сре́дствами</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on ne <b>brézgujet</b> nikakími srédstvami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he does not scruple/disdain to use any means; he is not squeamish/fastidious about any means he uses</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брезгливый.html>брезгли́вый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">brezglívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брезгливость.html>брезгли́вость</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">brezglívostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><b>бре́з<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>го<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 2a.
<a href = vnd.unilang:участник.html>Уча́стники</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ситуация.html>ситуа́ции</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:описываемый.html>опи́сываемой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощью</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:брезговать.html>бре́зговать</a></i>: <img alt="NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg/24px-NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg.png" decoding="async" width="24" height="24" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg/36px-NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg/48px-NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="75" data-file-height="75" /> <a href = vnd.unilang:субъект.html>субъект</a> (им. п.), <img alt="NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg/24px-NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="24" height="24" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg/36px-NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg/48px-NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="75" data-file-height="75" /> <a href = vnd.unilang:объект.html>объект</a> (твор. п.).

***брезент.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:брезент.html>брезе́нт</a> (6329)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the earlier form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">презенинг</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prezening</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">presenning</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">préceinte</i>. <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">presenning</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">brezent</i> derive from the same French word.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брезент.html>брезе́нт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">brezént</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брезент.html>брезе́нта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брезент.html>брезе́нты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брезент.html>брезе́нтов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брезентовый.html>брезе́нтовый</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tarpaulin, canvas</li></ol>

***брезжить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:брезжить.html>бре́зжить</a> (25592)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From dialectal <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">брезг</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brezg</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dawn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*brězgъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брезжить.html>бре́зжить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">brézžitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забрезжить.html>забре́зжить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also  impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dawn</li>
<li>to flicker faintly</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dawn, to emerge, to begin to manifest <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of hope, a thought, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><b>бре́з<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>жить</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:забрезжить.html>забре́зжить</a>.
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:существовать.html>Существу́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;">устар.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ниями</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наст.html>наст</a>. вр.: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:брезжить.html>бре́зжет</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:брезжить.html>бре́зжут</a></i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бремя.html>бре́мя</a> (12426)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">брѣмѧ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brěmę</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">брѣмѧ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brěmę</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bermę</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">load, burden</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*BʰerH-men-</i>. Compare the inherited doublet <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бере́мя</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">berémja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бремя.html>бре́мя</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">brémja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бремя.html>бре́мени</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <span class="hypothetical-star">*</span><i class="Cyrl hypothetical" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бремя.html>бремена́</a></i>, <i>genitive plural</i> <span class="hypothetical-star">*</span><i class="Cyrl hypothetical" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бремя.html>бремён</a></i>)
</p>
<ol><li>burden, charge, load
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большо́е</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бремя.html>бре́мя</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чего́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bolʹšóje <b>brémja</b> dlja čevó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">big <b>burden</b> for something</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> perishable, fleeting, mortal, frail

***бренчать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бренчать.html>бренча́ть</a> (18639)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Onomatopoeic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бренчать.html>бренча́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">brenčátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to jingle, to clink, to chink <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to make a noise of metal or glass clattering against itself</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to strum</li></ol>

***брести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:брести.html>брести́</a> (5422)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:брести.html>брести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bresti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*brestì</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰredʰ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брести.html>брести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">brestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <i>(concrete verb)</i>
</p>
<ol><li>to plod, to lag</li>
<li>to stroll</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:брести.html>Брести́</a></b> is a Russian concrete verb. Its counterpart, <a href = vnd.unilang:бродить.html>броди́ть</a>, is an abstract verb.
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брешь.html>брешь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">brešʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брехать.html>бре́ши</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брехать.html>бре́ши</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брешь.html>бре́шей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>breach, gap; break, tear</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:брешь.html>брешь</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 3-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 8a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бригада.html>брига́да</a> (1681)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Brigade</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бригада.html>брига́да</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">brigáda</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бригада.html>брига́ды</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бригада.html>брига́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бригада.html>брига́д</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>crew, team, gang <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">group of people employed to work together on a common task</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> brigade</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">criminal  slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gang, crew <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">group of criminals</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><b>бри<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:кан.html>ган</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ти.html>ти́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b>

***бриз.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бриз.html>бриз</a> (23118)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from some Western European language, most likely from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">breeze</i>. Further etymology unknown.
</p><p>Initially attested in 1718 in form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бриз.html>бри́зами</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brízami</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in the context of names of different kinds of winds in Portugal. This instrumental plural form is likely not from modern spelling <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бриз.html>бриз</a></i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">briz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, but from an exact rendering of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt">brisa</i>, which would be <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">*<a href = vnd.unilang:бриз.html>бри́за</a></i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*briza</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (both have identical case forms in plural).
</p><p>Judging by the lack of further attestations in the 18th century, the term didn't settle in the language until 19th century (and from a different source).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бриз.html>бриз</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">briz</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бриз.html>бри́за</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бриз.html>бри́зы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бриз.html>бри́зов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sea breeze</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бриз.html>бриз</a></b>
